 ) kaamanwealth games ke aayojan main hui aniyamittaaon main pradhanmantri karyaalay ko sanlipt karte hue niyantrak or mahalekha pareekshak (kaig) ne apni report main kaha ki gambhir virodh ke baavjood piemo ke kehane par suresh kalmadi ko aayojan samiti kaa pramukh niyukti kiya gaya

 kaig ne apni report main yah bhi kaha ki kaha ki soche-samajhe uddeshy ke tahat kritrim jaldbaaji kaa maahaul banaaya gaya

 kaig ne yah bhi kaha ki rashtramandal khelon main aayojan samiti kii mukhya bhoomika thi, lekin is samiti ne jin vyaktiyon ko pramukh jimmedaariyaan saunpi thim, unke paas itane vishaal str kii jimmedaariyon ko nibhaane kii na to yogyata thi or na hi anubhav
 CAG said in its report that most of the appointments were arbitrary by the organizing committee, that the committee did not even take care of standard appointment procedures such as advertisements for posts, selection committees, security clearances etc
 kaig ne apni report main kaha ki disambar, 2004 main tatkaaleen khelmantri sunil dutt ke gambhir virodh ke baavjood pradhanmantri karyaalay kii sifarish ke aadhaar par suresh kalmadi ko aayojan samiti kaa adhyaksh bana diya gaya

 In today's hearing, the Supreme Court Chief Justice JS Khehar asked Salman Khurshid, who is playing the role of amicus curiae in the case, whether triple talaq is just a practice in Islam or is it an integral part of Islam? The Constitution Bench wanted to know whether any such custom which is a crime can be a part of Sharia? The Supreme Court also asked Khurshid whether any crime can be considered as the will of God or whether it would be more right to call it a law made by humans? The judges asked that the practice of triple talaq is prevalent outside India also? The court wanted to know how this practice ended in other countries? The court held that triple talaq is the 'worst' and 'undesirable' way of ending the relationship between husband and wife in Islam
 haalanki samvidhan peeth ne sweekaar kiya ki islam kii kai vichaardhaaraein ise jaij maanati hai
 Khurshid's reply Khurshid told the court that in the eyes of the All India Muslim Personal Law Board, divorce is a disgusting but valid custom
 khurshid kaa kahana tha ki unki nijee raay main teen talaak 'paap' he or islam kisi bhi gunaah kii ijaajat nahin de saktaa
 In response to questions from the bench, Khurshid said that a crime like triple talaq cannot be part of the Shariah
 unhone bataaya ki sirf bhartiya muslimon main hi teen talaak kaa prachlan he
 Khurshid suggested that saying divorce thrice together should be considered a single declaration of divorce
 unki raay main agar teen talaak ko 'ek talaak' mana jayega to ise palatnaa aasaan hoga
 Khurshid said that what is happening in India now has already happened abroad
 isi ke chalate kai deshon main teen talaak kii pratha ko khatm kar diya gaya he
 Salman Khurshid said that according to Islamic law, a woman can put a condition in the Nikahnama according to which she should be allowed to say 'no' to the three divorces

 According to the court, he will first decide whether this practice is a fundamental part of Islam or not? If it can, can it be enforced under the Fundamental Rights? The court has made it clear that if the constitution bench comes to the conclusion that triple talaq is a fundamental part of Islam, then it will not look into the question of its constitutional validity
